 bharat main 1952 se 2014 ke bich 668 adhyadesh jari kiye gaye hai

 kai adhyadesh to 13 saal tak jari hote rahe

 duusare rajyon kaa adhyayan ho to vahaan bhi yahi tasviir niklegi

 phir bijepi ke netaa khud se hi hamale karne lage

 maa-bete kii sarkaar to yaad hi hoga

 Railway ticket booking site IRCTC has launched a new facility 'e-wallet' for the convenience of its users
 yah ek virtual wolet kii tarah kaam karata he, jiskaa istemaal yujar tikat shulk adaa karne ke liye kar paaegaa
 That is, now the user will not need debit, credit card or internet banking to pay the ticket money
 kya he i-woleti-wolet iarsitsi kii site par uplabdh ek tarah kaa online preeped acount he, jisamen aap tikat booking ke liye rupee jamaa kar sakate hai
 If needed, those money can be used to pay the ticket fee
 ab jaldi book hoga aapkaa tiktais preeped acanut kii suvidha se ab aapkaa tikat pehle ke mukaable jaldi book ho sakegaa
 It is just like your common bank account, where you use the money already deposited for shopping
 fark sirf itnaa he ki 'i-wolet' main jamaa rupee kaa istemaal aap sirf iarsitisi kii site par hi kar paaenge
 How to register for e-wallet: If you want to use e-wallet to book tickets, then you have to register for e-wallet
 yahaan aapako apane pan card kaa number or apane naam kaa pehla shabd tip karnaa hota he
 After this, an online form will open in front of you, where you can create your password by transferring money for e-wallet
 aap i-wolet kaa istemaal iarsitisi kii site par kisi anya product kii kharidari ke liye bhi kar sakate hai
 You can deposit from Rs 100 to Rs 5000 in e-wallet
 kaise karenge istemalonline shopping or tikat booking ke liye i-wolet kii suvidha lene ke liye site par login ke baad product yaa tikat salect kar pement opshan main aapako i-wolet par clic karnaa hoga
 Where after entering your transition password, you will be able to use the deposited money
 i-wolet se phydabhi tak ham iarsitisi par tikat book karne ke liye jin pement opshan kaa istemaal karte the, usamen pement ke liye site ko sambandhit bank se online judana or getwe pement bank ke sarvapar par janaa hota tha
 It takes a lot of time and sometimes the payment fails
 lekin ab is nai suvidha se iarsitisi ko apane hi site se pement lenaa hoga, yani samay kii bachat hogi
 Even in the event of cancellation of the ticket, refunded money will soon come to your e-wallet account
 haalanki i-wolet kaa istemaal aap iarsitisi par tikat book karne ke liye subah 8:00 se 12:00 baje tak nahin kar paaenge

 What is Section 376 of the IPC The accused of raping any woman is tried under Section 376 of the IPC
 aparaadh siddh ho jane par doshi ko nunatam 7 saal or adhiktam 10 saal kii kadi sajaa die jane kaa praavdhaan he
 In many rare cases, the convict can also be sentenced to life imprisonment
 iske alaava jurmaana lagaaya ja saktaa he

 Why is Friendship Day celebrated on the first Sunday of August? 
 Let's know what is the history of Friendship Day- This day, celebrated as a symbol of friendship, was first started in 1919 by Hall Hall Card founder Jose Hall, who suggested celebrating friendship
 - 1935 main pehali baar united stats congress ne agast ke pehle ravivaar ko friendship de manaane kii ghoshnaa kii thi
 - It was first celebrated in America
 - is avasar par doston ko friendship band, card, gifts die jate hai
 Friendship Day: These 5 films based on friendship will make emotional - tell you, in 1997, Miln's cartoon character Vinny the Pooh was chosen by the United Nations as the international ambassador for friendship
 - bharat main agast ke pehle ravivaar ko friendship de manaaya jaataa he, lekin dakshin america deshon main july maheene ko kaaphi paavan mana jaataa he
 Therefore, this day is celebrated in late July
 bangladesh or malaysia main digital communications ke tahat yah din zyada charchit ho gaya he
 The United Nations also stamped on this day
 - media report ke mutabik america deshon main yah samay aisa hota he, jab dur-dur tak kisi parv-tyohaar kii chuttee nahin hoti
 On July 30 of 1958, International Friendship Day (world Friendship Day) was formally announced
 - kareeb 60 saal pehle 1958 main pehali baar friendship de ko antarrashtriya manyata praapt hui jab dakshin america ke kai desh khaastaur par paragave main friendship de manaaya gaya
